```python
def remove_matching_tuple(tuple1, tuple2):
    # Convert tuples to sets for efficient removal of duplicates
    set1 = set(tuple1)
    set2 = set(tuple2)
    
    # Find the intersection of both sets to get matching tuples
    matching_tuples = set1.intersection(set2)
    
    # Remove the matching tuples from the original tuples
    tuple1 = tuple([item for item in tuple1 if item not in matching_tuples])
    tuple2 = tuple([item for item in tuple2 if item not in matching_tuples])
    
    return tuple1, tuple2
```

def occurance_substring(text, substring):
    occurrences = []
    start = 0
    while True:
        pos = text.find(substring, start)
        if pos == -1:
            break
        occurrences.append((pos, pos + len(substring) - 1))
        start = pos + 1
    return occurrences
```

    occurrences = []
    start = 0
    while True:
        pos = text.find(substring, start)
        if pos == -1:
            break
        occurrences.append((pos, pos + len(substring) - 1))
        start = pos + 1
    return occurrences

def modified_encode(lst):
    result = []
    count = 1
    for i in range(1, len(lst)):
        if lst[i] == lst[i-1]:
            count += 1
        else:
            result.append((count, lst[i-1]))
            count = 1
    result.append((count, lst[-1]))  # Append the last group
    return result

Task 714 raw output:
```python
def count_Fac(n):
    # Initialize a counter for the number of distinct prime factors
    count = 0
    
    # Divide n by 2 until it's odd
    while n % 2 == 0:
        count += 1
        n //= 2
    
    # Check for odd factors from 3 onwards
    i = 3
    while i * i <= n:
        if n % i == 0:
            count += 1
            n //= i
        else:
            i += 2
    
    # If n is a prime number greater than 2
    if n > 2:
        count += 1
    
    return count
```
Task 714 generated code:
def count_Fac(n):
    # Initialize a counter for the number of distinct prime factors
    count = 0
    
    # Divide n by 2 until it's odd
    while n % 2 == 0:
        count += 1
        n //= 2
    
    # Check for odd factors from 3 onwards
    i = 3
    while i * i <= n:
        if n % i == 0:
            count += 1
            n //= i
        else:
            i += 2
    
    # If n is a prime number greater than 2
    if n > 2:
        count += 1
    
    return count

def count_element_freq(mixed_tuple):
    freq_dict = {}
    for item in mixed_tuple:
        if isinstance(item, (list, tuple)):
            freq_dict.update(count_element_freq(item))
        else:
            freq_dict[item] = freq_dict.get(item, 0) + 1
    return freq_dict

def sum_Pairs(arr):
    arr.sort()  # Sort the array to make it easier to calculate the sum of absolute differences
    total_sum = 0
    for i in range(len(arr)):
        total_sum += (arr[i] * (len(arr) - i - 1)) - (arr[i] * i)
    return total_sum

```python
import re

def find_literals(literals, text):
    # Define the regular expression pattern for literals
    pattern = r'\b' + literals + r'\b'
    
    # Find all occurrences of the literal in the text
    matches = re.findall(pattern, text)
    
    if matches:
        return [match[0] for match in matches], [text.index(match) for match in matches]
    else:
        return [], []
```

import re

def find_literals(literals, text):
    # Define the regular expression pattern for literals
    pattern = r'\b' + literals + r'\b'

    matches = re.findall(pattern, text)
    
    if matches:
        return [match[0] for match in matches], [text.index(match) for match in matches]
    else:
        return [], []

```python
def binomial_coefficient(n, k):
    # Initialize the result as 1 (since any number multiplied by 1 remains unchanged)
    result = 1
    
    # Calculate the factorial of n and divide it by the product of (n-k) and k!
    for i in range(1, min(k+1, n-k+1)):
        result *= (n - i + 1) // i
        
    return result
```
Task 28 generated code:
def binomial_coefficient(n, k):
    # Initialize the result as 1 (since any number multiplied by 1 remains unchanged)
    result = 1
    
    # Calculate the factorial of n and divide it by the product of (n-k) and k!
    for i in range(1, min(k+1, n-k+1)):
        result *= (n - i + 1) // i
        
    return result

def largest_palindrome(arr):
    # Sort the array in descending order
    arr.sort(reverse=True)
    
    # Iterate through the sorted array to find the largest palindrome
    for i in range(len(arr)):
        for j in range(i, len(arr)):
            if str(arr[i]) == str(arr[j])[::-1]:
                return arr[i]
```

```python
def max_sub_array_sum(nums):
    if not nums:
        return 0
    
    max_sum = current_sum = nums[0]
    
    for num in nums[1:]:
        current_sum = max(num, current_sum + num)
        max_sum = max(max_sum, current_sum)
    
    return max_sum
```
Task 836 generated code:
def max_sub_array_sum(nums):
    if not nums:
        return 0
    
    max_sum = current_sum = nums[0]
    
    for num in nums[1:]:
        current_sum = max(num, current_sum + num)
        max_sum = max(max_sum, current_sum)
    
    return max_sum

def get_Number(arr, k):
    # Initialize pointers for odd and even indices
    odd_index = 0
    even_index = len(arr) - 1
    
    # Loop until we find the kth element
    while odd_index <= even_index:
        if arr[odd_index] % 2 != 0:  # If current odd index is not the kth element
            odd_index += 1
        elif arr[even_index] % 2 == 0:  # If current even index is not the kth element
            even_index -= 1
        else:  # If both indices are the kth element, return it
            return arr[k - 1]

def median_trapezium(a, b, c, d):
    """
    Calculate the median of a trapezium given its four vertices.
    
    Args:
    a (float): The x-coordinate of vertex A.
    b (float): The y-coordinate of vertex A.
    c (float): The x-coordinate of vertex C.
    d (float): The y-coordinate of vertex C.
    
    Returns:
    float: The median of the trapezium.
    """
    # Calculate the lengths of the parallel sides
    side1 = abs(c - a)
    side2 = abs(d - b)
    
    # Calculate the height of the trapezium
    height = abs(b - d) / 2
    
    # Calculate the median using the formula for the median of a trapezium
    median = (side1 + side2) * height / 2

    """
    Calculate the median of a trapezium given its four vertices.
    
    Args:
    a (float): The x-coordinate of vertex A.
    b (float): The y-coordinate of vertex A.

        # Calculate the sum of digits of the current number

def max_difference(pairs):
    # Sort the pairs based on the second element of each pair
    sorted_pairs = sorted(pairs, key=lambda x: x[1])
    
    # Initialize the maximum difference to 0
    max_diff = 0
    
    # Iterate through the sorted pairs
    for i in range(len(sorted_pairs) - 1):
        # Calculate the difference between consecutive pairs
        diff = sorted_pairs[i + 1][1] - sorted_pairs[i][0]
        
        # Update the maximum difference if the current difference is greater
        max_diff = max(max_diff, diff)
    
    return max_diff

```python
def modular_sum(arr, n, m):
    # Initialize a boolean array to store the results of subproblems
    dp = [[False] * (m + 1) for _ in range(n + 1)]
    
    # Base case: There is always a subset with sum 0
    dp[0][0] = True
    
    # Fill the dp table
    for i in range(1, n + 1):
        for j in range(1, m + 1):
            if arr[i - 1] <= j:
                dp[i][j] = dp[i - 1][j] or dp[i - 1][j - arr[i - 1]]
            else:
                dp[i][j] = dp[i - 1][j]
    
    # Check if there is a subset with sum divisible by m
    return dp[n][m]
```
Task 515 generated code:
def modular_sum(arr, n, m):
    # Initialize a boolean array to store the results of subproblems
    dp = [[False] * (m + 1) for _ in range(n + 1)]
    
    # Base case: There is always a subset with sum 0
    dp[0][0] = True
    
    # Fill the dp table
    for i in range(1, n + 1):
        for j in range(1, m + 1):
            if arr[i - 1] <= j:
                dp[i][j] = dp[i - 1][j] or dp[i - 1][j - arr[i - 1]]
            else:
                dp[i][j] = dp[i - 1][j]
    
    # Check if there is a subset with sum divisible by m
    return dp[n][m]

def count_Fac(n):
    # Initialize count to 0
    count = 0
    
    # Divide n by 2 until it's odd
    while n % 2 == 0:
        count += 1
        n //= 2
    
    # Check for odd factors starting from 3
    i = 3
    while i * i <= n:
        if n % i == 0:
            count += 1
            n //= i
        else:
            i += 2
    
    # If n is a prime number greater than 2
    if n > 2:
        count += 1
    
    return count
```

def intersection_nested_lists(list1, list2):
    # Convert both lists to sets for efficient lookup
    set1 = set(list1)
    set2 = set(list2)
    
    # Find the intersection of the two sets
    common_elements = set1.intersection(set2)
    
    # Convert the result back to a list and return it
    return [element for element in list1 if element in common_elements]

def binomial_Coeff(n, k):
    # Initialize the result as 1 (since any number multiplied by 1 remains unchanged)
    result = 1
    
    # Calculate the factorial of n and divide it by the product of (n-k) and k!
    for i in range(1, min(k+1, n-k+1)):
        result *= (n-i) // i
        
    return result

    def is_palindrome(num):
        return str(num) == str(num)[::-1]

def max_sub_array_sum(nums, k):
    if not nums or k <= 0:
        return 0
    
    current_sum = max_sum = 0
    start = 0
    
    for end in range(len(nums)):
        current_sum += nums[end]
        
        while current_sum > k and start <= end:
            current_sum -= nums[start]
            start += 1
        
        max_sum = max(max_sum, current_sum)
    
    return max_sum

def get_Number(arr, k):
    # Initialize pointers for odd and even indices
    odd_index = 0
    even_index = len(arr) - 1
    
    while odd_index < even_index:
        # If the current element is odd, move to the next odd index
        if arr[odd_index] % 2 != 0:
            odd_index += 1
        # If the current element is even, swap it with the element at the even index
        else:
            arr[odd_index], arr[even_index] = arr[even_index], arr[odd_index]
            even_index -= 1
    
    # Return the kth element in the array
    return arr[k-1]
```

    # Flatten the matrix by transposing it and then converting each row to a tuple

```python
def count_Fac(n):
    def is_prime(num):
        if num <= 1:
            return False
        for i in range(2, int(num**0.5) + 1):
            if num % i == 0:
                return False
        return True

    prime_factors = set()
    while n > 1:
        for i in range(2, n + 1):
            if is_prime(i) and n % i == 0:
                prime_factors.add(i)
                n //= i
                break
    return len(prime_factors)
```
Task 714 generated code:
def count_Fac(n):
    def is_prime(num):
        if num <= 1:
            return False
        for i in range(2, int(num**0.5) + 1):
            if num % i == 0:
                return False
        return True

    prime_factors = set()
    while n > 1:
        for i in range(2, n + 1):
            if is_prime(i) and n % i == 0:
                prime_factors.add(i)
                n //= i
                break
    return len(prime_factors)

def max_sub_array_sum(nums):
    if not nums:
        return 0
    
    current_max = global_max = nums[0]
    
    for num in nums[1:]:
        current_max = max(num, current_max + num)
        global_max = max(global_max, current_max)
    
    return global_max

    # Initialize pointers for odd and even indices
    odd_index = 0
    even_index = len(arr) - 1
    
    # Traverse the array from both ends towards the center
    while odd_index <= even_index:
        # If the current element is odd, move to the next odd index
        if arr[odd_index] % 2 != 0:
            odd_index += 1
        # If the current element is even, move to the previous even index
        elif arr[even_index] % 2 == 0:
            even_index -= 1
        else:
            # If both elements are odd or even, return the kth element
            if k <= odd_index:
                return arr[k]
            else:
                return arr[even_index]

```python
def modular_sum(arr, n, m):
    # Check if the total sum of the array is divisible by m
    if (sum(arr) % m != 0):
        return False
    
    # Initialize a boolean array to store whether a subset with sum i exists or not
    dp = [False] * (m + 1)
    
    # Base case: There is always a subset with sum 0 (empty set)
    dp[0] = True
    
    # Fill the dp array
    for num in arr:
        for i in range(m, num - 1, -1):
            dp[i] = dp[i] or dp[i - num]
    
    return dp[m]
```
Task 515 generated code:
def modular_sum(arr, n, m):
    # Check if the total sum of the array is divisible by m
    if (sum(arr) % m != 0):
        return False
    
    # Initialize a boolean array to store whether a subset with sum i exists or not
    dp = [False] * (m + 1)
    
    # Base case: There is always a subset with sum 0 (empty set)
    dp[0] = True
    
    # Fill the dp array
    for num in arr:
        for i in range(m, num - 1, -1):
            dp[i] = dp[i] or dp[i - num]
    
    return dp[m]

def count_Fac(n):
    def is_prime(num):
        if num <= 1:
            return False
        for i in range(2, int(num**0.5) + 1):
            if num % i == 0:
                return False
        return True

    prime_factors = set()
    divisor = 2
    while n > 1:
        while n % divisor == 0:
            prime_factors.add(divisor)
            n //= divisor
        divisor += 1
    return len(prime_factors)
```

    if not nums or k <= 0:
        return 0
    
    current_sum = max_sum = nums[0]
    
    for i in range(1, len(nums)):
        current_sum = max(nums[i], current_sum + nums[i])
        max_sum = max(max_sum, current_sum)
        
        if i >= k:
            current_sum -= nums[i - k]
    
    return max_sum

def get_Number(arr, k):
    # Initialize pointers for odd and even indices
    odd_index = 0
    even_index = len(arr) - 1
    
    # Traverse the array from both ends towards the center
    while odd_index < even_index:
        # If current element is odd, move to the next odd index
        if arr[odd_index] % 2 != 0:
            odd_index += 1
        # If current element is even, move to the previous even index
        else:
            even_index -= 1
    
    # Return the kth element (which will be at the even index)
    return arr[even_index]
```

```python
def modular_sum(arr, n, m):
    dp = [[False] * (m + 1) for _ in range(n + 1)]
    
    # Initialize the base case
    dp[0][0] = True
    
    # Fill the DP table
    for i in range(1, n + 1):
        for j in range(1, m + 1):
            if arr[i - 1] <= j:
                dp[i][j] = dp[i - 1][j] or dp[i - 1][j - arr[i - 1]]
            else:
                dp[i][j] = dp[i - 1][j]
    
    return dp[n][m]
```
Task 515 generated code:
def modular_sum(arr, n, m):
    dp = [[False] * (m + 1) for _ in range(n + 1)]
    
    # Initialize the base case
    dp[0][0] = True
    
    # Fill the DP table
    for i in range(1, n + 1):
        for j in range(1, m + 1):
            if arr[i - 1] <= j:
                dp[i][j] = dp[i - 1][j] or dp[i - 1][j - arr[i - 1]]
            else:
                dp[i][j] = dp[i - 1][j]
    
    return dp[n][m]

```python
def count_Fac(n):
    def is_prime(num):
        if num <= 1:
            return False
        for i in range(2, int(num**0.5) + 1):
            if num % i == 0:
                return False
        return True

    prime_factors = set()
    while n > 1:
        for i in range(2, n + 1):
            if is_prime(i) and n % i == 0:
                prime_factors.add(i)
                n //= i
                break
    return len(prime_factors)
```

    def is_prime(num):
        if num <= 1:
            return False

                return False

    prime_factors = set()
    while n > 1:

    left, right = 0, len(sorted_list)

        mid = (left + right) // 2

    if not arr:
        return 0
    
    max_current = max_global = arr[0]
    
    for num in arr[1:]:
        max_current = max(num, max_current + num)
        max_global = max(max_global, max_current)
    
    return max_global

```python
def get_Number(arr, k):
    # Initialize pointers for odd and even indices
    odd_index = 0
    even_index = len(arr) - 1
    
    # Traverse the array from both ends towards the center
    while odd_index <= even_index:
        # If the current element is odd, move to the next odd index
        if arr[odd_index] % 2 != 0:
            odd_index += 1
        # If the current element is even, move to the previous even index
        elif arr[even_index] % 2 == 0:
            even_index -= 1
        else:
            # If both elements are odd or even, return the kth element
            return arr[k - 1]
    
    # If k is out of bounds, return None
    return None
```

import re

def find_literals(text, pattern):
    matches = re.finditer(pattern, text)
    start_positions = [match.start() for match in matches]
    end_positions = [match.end() for match in matches]
    return (pattern, min(start_positions), max(end_positions))

def max_sub_array_sum(nums, k):
    if not nums or k <= 0:
        return 0
    
    current_sum = max_sum = nums[0]
    
    for i in range(1, len(nums)):
        current_sum = max(nums[i], current_sum + nums[i])
        max_sum = max(max_sum, current_sum)
        
        if i >= k:
            current_sum -= nums[i - k]
            
    return max_sum

```python
def get_Number(arr, k):
    # Initialize pointers for odd and even indices
    odd_index = 0
    even_index = len(arr) - 1
    
    # Traverse the array from both ends towards the center
    while odd_index < even_index:
        # If the current element is odd, move to the next odd index
        if arr[odd_index] % 2 != 0:
            odd_index += 1
        # If the current element is even, move to the previous even index
        else:
            even_index -= 1
    
    # Return the kth element (which will be at the odd_index)
    return arr[odd_index]
```

    n = len(arr)

            if num % i == 0:
                return False

def max_sub_array_sum(arr):
    max_current = max_global = arr[0]
    start = end = 0
    temp_start = 0

    for i in range(1, len(arr)):
        if arr[i] > max_current + arr[i]:
            max_current = arr[i]
            temp_start = i
        else:
            max_current += arr[i]

        if max_current > max_global:
            max_global = max_current
            start = temp_start
            end = i

    return end - start + 1
```

def min_Swaps(s1, s2):
    if len(s1) != len(s2):
        raise ValueError("Strings must be of the same length")
    
    diff = [i for i in range(len(s1)) if s1[i] != s2[i]]
    
    if len(diff) % 2 != 0:
        return -1
    
    swaps = 0
    for i in range(0, len(diff), 2):
        if diff[i+1] != diff[i] + 1:
            return -1
        swaps += 1
    
    return swaps // 2
```

def count_Fac(n):
    def is_prime(num):
        if num <= 1:
            return False
        for i in range(2, int(num**0.5) + 1):
            if num % i == 0:
                return False
        return True

    factors = set()
    for i in range(2, n + 1):
        if n % i == 0 and is_prime(i):
            factors.add(i)
    return len(factors)

def max_sub_array_sum(arr):
    max_current = max_global = arr[0]
    start = end = 0
    temp_start = 0

    for i in range(1, len(arr)):
        if arr[i] > max_current + arr[i]:
            max_current = arr[i]
            temp_start = i
        else:
            max_current += arr[i]

        if max_current > max_global:
            max_global = max_current
            start = temp_start
            end = i

    return end - start + 1
```

def count_Fac(n):
    def is_prime(num):
        if num <= 1:
            return False
        for i in range(2, int(num**0.5) + 1):
            if num % i == 0:
                return False
        return True

    prime_factors = set()
    for i in range(2, n + 1):
        while n % i == 0 and is_prime(i):
            prime_factors.add(i)
            n //= i
    return len(prime_factors)
```

    def is_prime(num):
        if num <= 1:

                return False
        return True

    prime_factors = set()

            prime_factors.add(i)

def max_sub_array_sum(arr):
    max_current = max_global = arr[0]
    start = end = 0
    temp_start = 0

    for i in range(1, len(arr)):
        if arr[i] > max_current + arr[i]:
            max_current = arr[i]
            temp_start = i
        else:
            max_current += arr[i]

        if max_current > max_global:
            max_global = max_current
            start = temp_start
            end = i

    return end - start + 1
```

def count_Fac(n):
    def is_prime(num):
        if num <= 1:
            return False
        for i in range(2, int(num**0.5) + 1):
            if num % i == 0:
                return False
        return True

    prime_factors = set()
    for i in range(2, n + 1):
        while n % i == 0 and is_prime(i):
            prime_factors.add(i)
            n //= i
    return len(prime_factors)
```

def count_Fac(n):
    def is_prime(num):
        if num <= 1:
            return False

                return False
        return True

    prime_factors = set()
    for i in range(2, n + 1):

            prime_factors.add(i)
            n //= i
    return len(prime_factors)

```python
def modular_sum(arr, m):
    n = len(arr)
    dp = [False] * m
    for num in arr:
        if dp[0]:
            return True
        temp = [False] * m
        for i in range(m):
            if dp[i]:
                temp[(i + num) % m] = True

Task 515 generated code:
def modular_sum(arr, m):
    n = len(arr)
    dp = [False] * m
    for num in arr:
        if dp[0]:
            return True
        temp = [False] * m
        for i in range(m):
            if dp[i]:
                temp[(i + num) % m] = True
        dp[num % m] = True
        dp = [a or b for a, b in zip(dp, temp)]
    return dp[0]

            encoded.append((current_element, count))
            current_element = element

    encoded.append((current_element, count))
    
    return [(element, count) if count > 1 else element for element, count in encoded]

```python
def count_Fac(n):
    def prime_factors(n):
        i = 2
        factors = set()
        while i * i <= n:
            if n % i:
                i += 1
            else:
                n //= i
                factors.add(i)
        if n > 1:
            factors.add(n)
        return factors

    def count_distinct_powers(factors):
        powers = set()
        for factor in factors:
            power = 0
            while n % factor == 0:
                n //= factor
                power += 1
            if power > 0:
                powers.add((factor, power))
        return len(powers)

    factors = prime_factors(n)
    return count_distinct_powers(factors)
```

def intersection_nested_lists(list1, list2):
    def flatten(lst):
        for item in lst:
            if isinstance(item, list):
                yield from flatten(item)
            else:
                yield item

    flat_list1 = set(flatten(list1))
    flat_list2 = set(flatten(list2))
    
    return list(flat_list1 & flat_list2)

def max_sub_array_sum(nums):
    if not nums:
        return 0

    max_sum = current_sum = start = end = temp_start = 0

    for i in range(len(nums)):
        if current_sum + nums[i] > nums[i]:
            current_sum += nums[i]
        else:
            current_sum = nums[i]
            temp_start = i

        if current_sum > max_sum:
            max_sum = current_sum
            start = temp_start
            end = i

    return end - start + 1
```

def min_Swaps(s1, s2):
    if len(s1) != len(s2):
        return -1
    
    count_0s_s1 = 0
    count_1s_s2 = 0
    
    for i in range(len(s1)):
        if s1[i] == '0' and s2[i] == '1':
            count_0s_s1 += 1
        elif s1[i] == '1' and s2[i] == '0':
            count_1s_s2 += 1
    
    swaps = (count_0s_s1 + 1) // 2 + (count_1s_s2 + 1) // 2
    
    if (count_0s_s1 % 2 != count_1s_s2 % 2):
        return -1
    
    return swaps
```

def min_Swaps(str1, str2):
    if len(str1) != len(str2):
        return "Not Possible"
    
    count_01 = 0
    count_10 = 0
    
    for i in range(len(str1)):
        if str1[i] == '0' and str2[i] == '1':
            count_01 += 1
        elif str1[i] == '1' and str2[i] == '0':
            count_10 += 1
    
    if (count_01 + count_10) % 2 != 0:
        return "Not Possible"
    
    return (count_01 // 2) + (count_10 // 2)

def modular_sum(arr, m):
    n = len(arr)
    dp = [False] * m
    for num in arr:
        if dp[0]:
            return True
        temp = []
        for i in range(m):
            if dp[i]:
                temp.append((i + num) % m)
        for val in temp:
            dp[val] = True
        dp[num % m] = True
    return dp[0]
```

```python
def count_Fac(n):
    def prime_factors(n):
        i = 2
        factors = set()
        while i * i <= n:
            if n % i:
                i += 1
            else:
                n //= i
                factors.add(i)
        if n > 1:
            factors.add(n)
        return factors

    def count_distinct_powers(n):
        factors = prime_factors(n)
        power_count = set()
        for factor in factors:
            power = 0
            temp_n = n
            while temp_n % factor == 0:
                temp_n //= factor
                power += 1
            power_count.add(power)
        return len(power_count)

    return count_distinct_powers(n)
```
Task 714 generated code:
def count_Fac(n):
    def prime_factors(n):
        i = 2
        factors = set()
        while i * i <= n:
            if n % i:
                i += 1
            else:
                n //= i
                factors.add(i)
        if n > 1:
            factors.add(n)
        return factors

    def count_distinct_powers(n):
        factors = prime_factors(n)
        power_count = set()
        for factor in factors:
            power = 0
            temp_n = n
            while temp_n % factor == 0:
                temp_n //= factor
                power += 1
            power_count.add(power)
        return len(power_count)

    return count_distinct_powers(n)

def intersection_nested_lists(list1, list2):
    def flatten(lst):
        for item in lst:
            if isinstance(item, list):
                yield from flatten(item)
            else:
                yield item

    flat_list1 = set(flatten(list1))
    flat_list2 = set(flatten(list2))
    
    return list(flat_list1 & flat_list2)
```

def max_sub_array_sum(nums):
    if not nums:
        return 0

    max_sum = current_sum = start = end = temp_start = 0

    for i in range(len(nums)):
        if current_sum + nums[i] > nums[i]:
            current_sum += nums[i]
        else:
            current_sum = nums[i]
            temp_start = i

        if current_sum > max_sum:
            max_sum = current_sum
            start = temp_start
            end = i

    return end - start + 1
```

def count_Fac(n):
    def prime_factors(n):

        factors = {}

            if n % i:
                i += 1

                n //= i
                if i in factors:
                    factors[i] += 1
                else:
                    factors[i] = 1
        if n > 1:
            factors[n] = 1
        return factors

    factors = prime_factors(n)
    count = 0
    for exponent in factors.values():
        count += 1
    return count

def modular_sum(arr, m):
    n = len(arr)
    dp = [False] * m
    for num in arr:
        if dp[0]:
            return True
        temp = []
        for i in range(m):
            if dp[i]:
                temp.append((i + num) % m)
        for val in temp:
            dp[val] = True
        dp[num % m] = True
    return dp[0]
```

        dp[num % m] = True
    return dp[0]

```python
def count_Fac(n):
    def prime_factors(n):
        i = 2
        factors = set()
        while i * i <= n:
            if n % i:
                i += 1
            else:
                n //= i
                factors.add(i)
        if n > 1:
            factors.add(n)
        return factors

    def count_distinct_powers(n):
        factors = prime_factors(n)
        power_count = set()
        for factor in factors:
            power = 0
            while n % factor == 0:
                n //= factor
                power += 1
            if power > 0:
                power_count.add(power)
        return len(power_count)

    return count_distinct_powers(n)
```
Task 714 generated code:
def count_Fac(n):
    def prime_factors(n):
        i = 2
        factors = set()
        while i * i <= n:
            if n % i:
                i += 1
            else:
                n //= i
                factors.add(i)
        if n > 1:
            factors.add(n)
        return factors

    def count_distinct_powers(n):
        factors = prime_factors(n)
        power_count = set()
        for factor in factors:
            power = 0
            while n % factor == 0:
                n //= factor
                power += 1
            if power > 0:
                power_count.add(power)
        return len(power_count)

    return count_distinct_powers(n)

def intersection_nested_lists(list1, list2):
    def flatten(lst):
        for item in lst:
            if isinstance(item, list):
                yield from flatten(item)
            else:
                yield item

def intersection_nested_lists(list1, list2):
    def flatten(lst):
        for item in lst:
            if isinstance(item, list):
                yield from flatten(item)
            else:
                yield item

    flat_list1 = set(flatten(list1))
    flat_list2 = set(flatten(list2))
    
    return [item for item in flat_list1 if item in flat_list2]

def max_sub_array_sum(nums):
    if not nums:
        return 0

    max_sum = current_sum = start = end = temp_start = 0

    for i, num in enumerate(nums):
        if current_sum + num > num:
            current_sum += num
        else:
            current_sum = num
            temp_start = i

        if current_sum > max_sum:
            max_sum = current_sum
            start = temp_start
            end = i

    return end - start + 1
```

def min_Swaps(s1, s2):
    if len(s1) != len(s2):
        return -1
    
    count_01 = 0
    count_10 = 0
    
    for i in range(len(s1)):
        if s1[i] == '0' and s2[i] == '1':
            count_01 += 1
        elif s1[i] == '1' and s2[i] == '0':
            count_10 += 1
    
    swaps = (count_01 // 2) + (count_10 // 2)
    
    if count_01 % 2 != count_10 % 2:
        return -1
    
    return swaps + (count_01 % 2)

def count_Fac(n):
    def prime_factors(n):
        i = 2
        factors = set()
        while i * i <= n:
            if n % i:
                i += 1
            else:
                n //= i
                factors.add(i)
        if n > 1:
            factors.add(n)
        return factors

    def count_powers(n):
        powers = set()
        for factor in prime_factors(n):
            power = 0
            while n % factor == 0:
                n //= factor
                power += 1
            powers.add(power)
        return len(powers)

    return count_powers(n)
```
Task 714 generated code:
def count_Fac(n):
    def prime_factors(n):
        i = 2
        factors = set()
        while i * i <= n:
            if n % i:
                i += 1
            else:
                n //= i
                factors.add(i)
        if n > 1:
            factors.add(n)
        return factors

    def count_powers(n):
        powers = set()
        for factor in prime_factors(n):
            power = 0
            while n % factor == 0:
                n //= factor
                power += 1
            powers.add(power)
        return len(powers)

    return count_powers(n)
